\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{normalized\_u64\_to\_f64()}{normalized\_u64\_to\_f64()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8c_aee878603775170bfda13233591eceec0} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8c_aee1f2f5fb05f4936184a23f4dda732c9}{static\+\_\+inline}} \mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8c_a94dab5770726ccbef8c7d026cfbdf8e5}{f64}} normalized\+\_\+u64\+\_\+to\+\_\+f64 (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8c_a3f7e2bcbb0b4c338f3c4f6c937cd4234}{u64}}}]{val}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Convert normalized \doxylink{yyjson_8c_a3f7e2bcbb0b4c338f3c4f6c937cd4234}{u64} (highest bit is 1) to \doxylink{yyjson_8c_a94dab5770726ccbef8c7d026cfbdf8e5}{f64}.

Some compiler (such as Microsoft Visual C++ 6.\+0) do not support converting number from \doxylink{yyjson_8c_a3f7e2bcbb0b4c338f3c4f6c937cd4234}{u64} to \doxylink{yyjson_8c_a94dab5770726ccbef8c7d026cfbdf8e5}{f64}. This function will first convert \doxylink{yyjson_8c_a3f7e2bcbb0b4c338f3c4f6c937cd4234}{u64} to \doxylink{yyjson_8c_a85cb35fbe5bf2961d7ad5f26814a91a2}{i64} and then to \doxylink{yyjson_8c_a94dab5770726ccbef8c7d026cfbdf8e5}{f64}, with {\ttfamily to nearest} rounding mode. \Hypertarget{yyjson_8c_ab64abbf58258c4e8451e8a3057345f9a}\index{yyjson.c@{yyjson.c}!null\_free@{null\_free}}
\index{null\_free@{null\_free}!yyjson.c@{yyjson.c}}

Get a token from JSON pointer string. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em ptr} & \mbox{[}in,out\mbox{]} in\+: string that points to current token prefix {\ttfamily /} out\+: string that points to next token prefix {\ttfamily /}, or string end \\
\hline
{\em end} & \mbox{[}in\mbox{]} end of the entire JSON Pointer string \\
\hline
{\em len} & \mbox{[}out\mbox{]} unescaped token length \\
\hline
{\em esc} & \mbox{[}out\mbox{]} number of escaped characters in this token \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
head of the token, or NULL if syntax error 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8c_aee1f2f5fb05f4936184a23f4dda732c9}{static\+\_\+inline}} \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} read\+\_\+hex\+\_\+u16 (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8c_a92c50087ca0e64fa93fc59402c55f8ca}{u8}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{cur}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8c_ace9d960e74685e2cd84b36132dbbf8aa}{u16}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{val}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Scans an escaped character sequence as a UTF-\/16 code unit (branchless). e.\+g. "{}\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}u005\+C"{} should pass "{}005\+C"{} as {\ttfamily cur}.

This requires the string has 4-\/byte zero padding. \Hypertarget{yyjson_8c_ae2c50c33e8663e8985150a3c19fb7774}\index{yyjson.c@{yyjson.c}!read\_inf@{read\_inf}}

Read a JSON string. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em ptr} & The head pointer of string before \textquotesingle{}"{}\textquotesingle{} prefix (inout). \\
\hline
{\em lst} & JSON last position. \\
\hline
{\em inv} & Allow invalid unicode. \\
\hline
{\em val} & The string value to be written. \\
\hline
{\em msg} & The error message pointer. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
Whether success. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8c_abb4ba1f891e94f62b208432ebd8c5a78} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8c_abfda9d5678260b541e86dcc759194581}{static\+\_\+noinline}} \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} skip\+\_\+spaces\+\_\+and\+\_\+comments (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8c_a92c50087ca0e64fa93fc59402c55f8ca}{u8}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{ptr}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Skips spaces and comments as many as possible.

It will return false in these cases\+:
\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item No character is skipped. The \textquotesingle{}end\textquotesingle{} pointer is set as input cursor.
\item \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} multiline comment is not closed. The \textquotesingle{}end\textquotesingle{} pointer is set as the head of this comment block. 
\end{DoxyEnumerate}函数调用图\+:

\Hypertarget{yyjson_8c_a1bffc016bf4de6ed068a372d284f013b}\index{yyjson.c@{yyjson.c}!yyjson\_alc\_dyn\_free@{yyjson\_alc\_dyn\_free}}
\index{yyjson\_alc\_dyn\_free@{yyjson\_alc\_dyn\_free}!yyjson.c@{yyjson.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{yyjson\_alc\_dyn\_free()}{yyjson\_alc\_dyn\_free()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8c_a1bffc016bf4de6ed068a372d284f013b} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{ittnotify__static_8h_a61af67d9d838a9497ca5b188dabc1aa0}{void}} yyjson\+\_\+alc\+\_\+dyn\+\_\+free (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__alc}{yyjson\+\_\+alc}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{alc}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Free a dynamic allocator which is created by {\ttfamily \doxylink{yyjson_8h_a6a90ae91b82c2e8d6665a28a691eee18}{yyjson\+\_\+alc\+\_\+dyn\+\_\+new()}}. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em alc} & The dynamic allocator to be destroyed. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\Hypertarget{yyjson_8c_a41b8614e2637e2989d657af207cfa6ae}\index{yyjson.c@{yyjson.c}!yyjson\_alc\_dyn\_new@{yyjson\_alc\_dyn\_new}}
\index{yyjson\_alc\_dyn\_new@{yyjson\_alc\_dyn\_new}!yyjson.c@{yyjson.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{yyjson\_alc\_dyn\_new()}{yyjson\_alc\_dyn\_new()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8c_a41b8614e2637e2989d657af207cfa6ae} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__alc}{yyjson\+\_\+alc}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} yyjson\+\_\+alc\+\_\+dyn\+\_\+new (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{ittnotify__static_8h_a61af67d9d838a9497ca5b188dabc1aa0}{void}}}]{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} dynamic allocator.

This allocator has a similar usage to the pool allocator above. However, when there is not enough memory, this allocator will dynamically request more memory using libc\textquotesingle{}s {\ttfamily malloc} function, and frees it all at once when it is destroyed.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
\doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} new dynamic allocator, or NULL if memory allocation failed. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
The returned value should be freed with {\ttfamily \doxylink{yyjson_8h_aaa9b7978e7b40e6d5d8d1cb3da0568d6}{yyjson\+\_\+alc\+\_\+dyn\+\_\+free()}}.
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
This Allocator is not thread-\/safe. 
\end{DoxyWarning}
函数调用图\+:
% FIG 79
\Hypertarget{yyjson_8c_a6431b215f6588983c01ea62e689d9a34}\index{yyjson.c@{yyjson.c}!yyjson\_alc\_pool\_init@{yyjson\_alc\_pool\_init}}
\index{yyjson\_alc\_pool\_init@{yyjson\_alc\_pool\_init}!yyjson.c@{yyjson.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{yyjson\_alc\_pool\_init()}{yyjson\_alc\_pool\_init()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8c_a6431b215f6588983c01ea62e689d9a34} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} yyjson\+\_\+alc\+\_\+pool\+\_\+init (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__alc}{yyjson\+\_\+alc}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{alc}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{ittnotify__static_8h_a61af67d9d838a9497ca5b188dabc1aa0}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{buf}{, }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{size}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} pool allocator uses fixed length pre-\/allocated memory.

This allocator may be used to avoid malloc/realloc calls. The pre-\/allocated memory should be held by the caller. The maximum amount of memory required to read a JSON can be calculated using the {\ttfamily \doxylink{yyjson_8h_ae511cac592355c2f60f170402b9d8dbf}{yyjson\+\_\+read\+\_\+max\+\_\+memory\+\_\+usage()}} function, but the amount of memory required to write a JSON cannot be directly calculated.

This is not a general-\/purpose allocator. It is designed to handle a single JSON data at a time. If it is used for overly complex memory tasks, such as parsing multiple JSON documents using the same allocator but releasing only a few of them, it may cause memory fragmentation, resulting in performance degradation and memory waste.


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em alc} & The allocator to be initialized. If this parameter is NULL, the function will fail and return false. If {\ttfamily buf} or {\ttfamily size} is invalid, this will be set to an empty allocator. \\
\hline
{\em buf} & The buffer memory for this allocator. If this parameter is NULL, the function will fail and return false. \\
\hline
{\em size} & The size of {\ttfamily buf}, in bytes. If this parameter is less than 8 words (32/64 bytes on 32/64-\/bit OS), the function will fail and return false. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
true if the {\ttfamily alc} has been successfully initialized.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example}

\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{//\ parse\ JSON\ with\ stack\ memory}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordtype}{char}\ buf[1024];}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__alc}{yyjson\_alc}}\ alc;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a6068c4293a2b35493b18421b9afbd3d5}{yyjson\_alc\_pool\_init}}(\&alc,\ buf,\ 1024);}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{const}\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}\ *\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacenlohmann_a8ba8c5483f73a36e716558571ff97d57}{json}}\ =\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}\{\(\backslash\)"{}name\(\backslash\)"{}:\(\backslash\)"{}Helvetica\(\backslash\)"{},\(\backslash\)"{}size\(\backslash\)"{}:16\}"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__doc}{yyjson\_doc}}\ *doc\ =\ \mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_acf234d21f0cb4b7fc89381ef25e9f0a8}{yyjson\_read\_opts}}(json,\ strlen(json),\ 0,\ \&alc,\ \mbox{\hyperlink{eabase_8h_a070d2ce7b6bb7e5c05602aa8c308d0c4}{NULL}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{//\ the\ memory\ of\ \`{}doc`\ is\ on\ the\ stack}}

\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
This Allocator is not thread-\/safe. 
\end{DoxyWarning}

\Hypertarget{yyjson_8c_a51a046bcd5baaa2470b116e9b124b2a9}\index{yyjson.c@{yyjson.c}!yyjson\_locate\_pos@{yyjson\_locate\_pos}}
\index{yyjson\_locate\_pos@{yyjson\_locate\_pos}!yyjson.c@{yyjson.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{yyjson\_locate\_pos()}{yyjson\_locate\_pos()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8c_a51a046bcd5baaa2470b116e9b124b2a9} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} yyjson\+\_\+locate\+\_\+pos (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{str}{, }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{len}{, }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{pos}{, }\item[{size\+\_\+t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{line}{, }\item[{size\+\_\+t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{col}{, }\item[{size\+\_\+t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{chr}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Locate the line and column number for a byte position in a string. This can be used to get better description for error position.


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em str} & The input string. \\
\hline
{\em len} & The byte length of the input string. \\
\hline
{\em pos} & The byte position within the input string. \\
\hline
{\em line} & \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} pointer to receive the line number, starting from 1. \\
\hline
{\em col} & \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} pointer to receive the column number, starting from 1. \\
\hline
{\em chr} & \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} pointer to receive the character index, starting from 0. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
true on success, false if {\ttfamily str} is NULL or {\ttfamily pos} is out of bounds. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
Line/column/character are calculated based on Unicode characters for compatibility with text editors. For multi-\/byte UTF-\/8 characters, the returned value may not directly correspond to the byte position. 
\end{DoxyNote}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8c_a73406064ef5542e41529a5d547d66205} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__val}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} yyjson\+\_\+merge\+\_\+patch (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__doc}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+doc}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{doc}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__val}{yyjson\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{orig}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__val}{yyjson\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{patch}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Creates and returns a merge-\/patched JSON value (RFC 7386). The memory of the returned value is allocated by the {\ttfamily doc}. Returns NULL if the patch could not be applied.

This function is recursive and may cause a stack overflow if the object level is too deep.

\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__doc}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+doc}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+doc\+\_\+new (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__alc}{yyjson\+\_\+alc}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{alc}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Creates and returns a new mutable JSON document, returns NULL on error. If allocator is NULL, the default allocator will be used. \Hypertarget{yyjson_8c_a32aac3da1cbd2d6a2fe8b997a3b31b35}\index{yyjson.c@{yyjson.c}!yyjson\_mut\_doc\_set\_str\_pool\_size@{yyjson\_mut\_doc\_set\_str\_pool\_size}}
\index{yyjson\_mut\_doc\_set\_str\_pool\_size@{yyjson\_mut\_doc\_set\_str\_pool\_size}!yyjson.c@{yyjson.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{yyjson\_mut\_doc\_set\_str\_pool\_size()}{yyjson\_mut\_doc\_set\_str\_pool\_size()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8c_a32aac3da1cbd2d6a2fe8b997a3b31b35} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+doc\+\_\+set\+\_\+str\+\_\+pool\+\_\+size (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__doc}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+doc}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{doc}{, }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{len}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Set the string pool size for a mutable document. This function does not allocate memory immediately, but uses the size when the next memory allocation is needed.

If the caller knows the approximate bytes of strings that the document needs to store (e.\+g. copy string with {\ttfamily yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+strcpy} function), setting a larger size can avoid multiple memory allocations and improve performance.


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em doc} & The mutable document. \\
\hline
{\em len} & The desired string pool size in bytes (total string length). \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
true if successful, false if size is 0 or overflow. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\Hypertarget{yyjson_8c_ac6cf7367ab4d7442cf38b7291f5bed32}\index{yyjson.c@{yyjson.c}!yyjson\_mut\_doc\_set\_val\_pool\_size@{yyjson\_mut\_doc\_set\_val\_pool\_size}}
\index{yyjson\_mut\_doc\_set\_val\_pool\_size@{yyjson\_mut\_doc\_set\_val\_pool\_size}!yyjson.c@{yyjson.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{yyjson\_mut\_doc\_set\_val\_pool\_size()}{yyjson\_mut\_doc\_set\_val\_pool\_size()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8c_ac6cf7367ab4d7442cf38b7291f5bed32} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+doc\+\_\+set\+\_\+val\+\_\+pool\+\_\+size (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__doc}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+doc}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{doc}{, }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{count}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Set the value pool size for a mutable document. This function does not allocate memory immediately, but uses the size when the next memory allocation is needed.

If the caller knows the approximate number of values that the document needs to store (e.\+g. create new value with {\ttfamily yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+xxx} functions), setting a larger size can avoid multiple memory allocations and improve performance.


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em doc} & The mutable document. \\
\hline
{\em count} & The desired value pool size (number of {\ttfamily \doxylink{structyyjson__mut__val}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+val}}). \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
true if successful, false if size is 0 or overflow. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\Hypertarget{yyjson_8c_ae4de975cdc066079b82e165d0f7c3276}\index{yyjson.c@{yyjson.c}!yyjson\_mut\_merge\_patch@{yyjson\_mut\_merge\_patch}}

\Hypertarget{yyjson_8c_a8a9810ca1ea917038b5a9f0f6e9bd0cb}\index{yyjson.c@{yyjson.c}!yyjson\_mut\_val\_write\_file@{yyjson\_mut\_val\_write\_file}}
\index{yyjson\_mut\_val\_write\_file@{yyjson\_mut\_val\_write\_file}!yyjson.c@{yyjson.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{yyjson\_mut\_val\_write\_file()}{yyjson\_mut\_val\_write\_file()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8c_a8a9810ca1ea917038b5a9f0f6e9bd0cb} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+val\+\_\+write\+\_\+file (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{path}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__val}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{val}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_afb7989387fc481f678e13325c18e6338}{yyjson\+\_\+write\+\_\+flag}}}]{flg}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__alc}{yyjson\+\_\+alc}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{alc}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__write__err}{yyjson\+\_\+write\+\_\+err}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{err}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Write a value to JSON file with options.

This function is thread-\/safe when\+:
\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item The file is not accessed by other threads.
\item The {\ttfamily val} is not modified by other threads.
\item The {\ttfamily alc} is thread-\/safe or NULL.
\end{DoxyEnumerate}


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em path} & The JSON file\textquotesingle{}s path. If this path is NULL or invalid, the function will fail and return false. If this file is not empty, the content will be discarded. \\
\hline
{\em val} & The mutable JSON root value. If this parameter is NULL, the function will fail and return NULL. \\
\hline
{\em flg} & The JSON write options. Multiple options can be combined with {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}} operator. 0 means no options. \\
\hline
{\em alc} & The memory allocator used by JSON writer. Pass NULL to use the libc\textquotesingle{}s default allocator. \\
\hline
{\em err} & \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} pointer to receive error information. Pass NULL if you don\textquotesingle{}t need error information. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
true if successful, false if an error occurs.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
On 32-\/bit operating system, files larger than 2GB may fail to write. 
\end{DoxyWarning}
函数调用图\+:
% FIG 93

\hline
{\em err} & \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} pointer to receive error information. Pass NULL if you don\textquotesingle{}t need error information. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

true if successful, false if an error occurs.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8c_aa81190c624ca865e34e8492c4987feef} 
char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+val\+\_\+write\+\_\+opts (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__val}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{val}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_afb7989387fc481f678e13325c18e6338}{yyjson\+\_\+write\+\_\+flag}}}]{flg}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__alc}{yyjson\+\_\+alc}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{alc}{, }\item[{size\+\_\+t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{len}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__write__err}{yyjson\+\_\+write\+\_\+err}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{err}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Write a value to JSON string with options.

This function is thread-\/safe when\+:
\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item The {\ttfamily val} is not modified by other threads.
\item The {\ttfamily alc} is thread-\/safe or NULL.
\end{DoxyEnumerate}


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em val} & The mutable JSON root value. If this parameter is NULL, the function will fail and return NULL. \\
\hline
{\em flg} & The JSON write options. Multiple options can be combined with {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}} operator. 0 means no options. \\
\hline
{\em alc} & The memory allocator used by JSON writer. Pass NULL to use the libc\textquotesingle{}s default allocator. \\
\hline
{\em len} & \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} pointer to receive output length in bytes (not including the null-\/terminator). Pass NULL if you don\textquotesingle{}t need length information. \\
\hline
{\em err} & \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} pointer to receive error information. Pass NULL if you don\textquotesingle{}t need error information. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
\doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} new JSON string, or NULL if an error occurs. This string is encoded as UTF-\/8 with a null-\/terminator. When it\textquotesingle{}s no longer needed, it should be freed with \doxylink{mimalloc-override_8h_a9d4b5df3530d1bc733070a4669ba6ebc}{free()} or alc-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}\doxylink{mimalloc-override_8h_a9d4b5df3530d1bc733070a4669ba6ebc}{free()}. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{yyjson\_mut\_write\_file()}{yyjson\_mut\_write\_file()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8c_ab19fc560c2de646ffdb06659db8d52af} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+write\+\_\+file (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{path}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__doc}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+doc}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{doc}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_afb7989387fc481f678e13325c18e6338}{yyjson\+\_\+write\+\_\+flag}}}]{flg}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__alc}{yyjson\+\_\+alc}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{alc}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__write__err}{yyjson\+\_\+write\+\_\+err}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{err}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Write a document to JSON file with options.

This function is thread-\/safe when\+:
\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item The file is not accessed by other threads.
\item The {\ttfamily doc} is not modified by other threads.
\item The {\ttfamily alc} is thread-\/safe or NULL.
\end{DoxyEnumerate}


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em path} & The JSON file\textquotesingle{}s path. If this path is NULL or invalid, the function will fail and return false. If this file is not empty, the content will be discarded. \\
\hline
{\em doc} & The mutable JSON document. If this doc is NULL or has no root, the function will fail and return false. \\
\hline
{\em flg} & The JSON write options. Multiple options can be combined with {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}} operator. 0 means no options. \\
\hline
{\em alc} & The memory allocator used by JSON writer. Pass NULL to use the libc\textquotesingle{}s default allocator. \\
\hline
{\em err} & \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} pointer to receive error information. Pass NULL if you don\textquotesingle{}t need error information. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
true if successful, false if an error occurs.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
On 32-\/bit operating system, files larger than 2GB may fail to write. 
\end{DoxyWarning}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8c_a43932e149602ddfcd9257648ea36e553} 
char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+write\+\_\+opts (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__doc}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+doc}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{doc}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_afb7989387fc481f678e13325c18e6338}{yyjson\+\_\+write\+\_\+flag}}}]{flg}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__alc}{yyjson\+\_\+alc}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{alc}{, }\item[{size\+\_\+t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{len}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__write__err}{yyjson\+\_\+write\+\_\+err}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{err}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Write a document to JSON string with options.

This function is thread-\/safe when\+:
\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item The {\ttfamily doc} is not modified by other threads.
\item The {\ttfamily alc} is thread-\/safe or NULL.
\end{DoxyEnumerate}


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em doc} & The mutable JSON document. If this doc is NULL or has no root, the function will fail and return false. \\
\hline
{\em flg} & The JSON write options. Multiple options can be combined with {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}} operator. 0 means no options. \\
\hline
{\em alc} & The memory allocator used by JSON writer. Pass NULL to use the libc\textquotesingle{}s default allocator. \\
\hline
{\em len} & \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} pointer to receive output length in bytes (not including the null-\/terminator). Pass NULL if you don\textquotesingle{}t need length information. \\
\hline
{\em err} & \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} pointer to receive error information. Pass NULL if you don\textquotesingle{}t need error information. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
\doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} new JSON string, or NULL if an error occurs. This string is encoded as UTF-\/8 with a null-\/terminator. When it\textquotesingle{}s no longer needed, it should be freed with \doxylink{mimalloc-override_8h_a9d4b5df3530d1bc733070a4669ba6ebc}{free()} or alc-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}\doxylink{mimalloc-override_8h_a9d4b5df3530d1bc733070a4669ba6ebc}{free()}. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
函数调用图\+:

const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} yyjson\+\_\+read\+\_\+number (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{dat}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__val}{yyjson\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{val}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a36af676813028c1360e8b343768f0e81}{yyjson\+\_\+read\+\_\+flag}}}]{flg}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__alc}{yyjson\+\_\+alc}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{alc}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__read__err}{yyjson\+\_\+read\+\_\+err}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{err}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Read a JSON number.

This function is thread-\/safe when data is not modified by other threads.


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em dat} & The JSON data (UTF-\/8 without BOM), null-\/terminator is required. If this parameter is NULL, the function will fail and return NULL. \\
\hline
{\em val} & The output value where result is stored. If this parameter is NULL, the function will fail and return NULL. The value will hold either \doxylink{test__malloc__compliance_8cpp_a36cb3b01d81ffd844bbbfb54003e06ec}{UINT} or SINT or \doxylink{fft_8h_a5821460e95a0800cf9f24c38915cbbde}{REAL} number; \\
\hline
{\em flg} & The JSON read options. Multiple options can be combined with {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}} operator. 0 means no options. Supports {\ttfamily YYJSON\+\_\+\+READ\+\_\+\+NUMBER\+\_\+\+AS\+\_\+\+RAW} and {\ttfamily YYJSON\+\_\+\+READ\+\_\+\+ALLOW\+\_\+\+INF\+\_\+\+AND\+\_\+\+NAN}. \\
\hline
{\em alc} & The memory allocator used for long number. It is only used when the built-\/in floating point reader is disabled. Pass NULL to use the libc\textquotesingle{}s default allocator. \\
\hline
{\em err} & \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} pointer to receive error information. Pass NULL if you don\textquotesingle{}t need error information. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
If successful, a pointer to the character after the last character used in the conversion, NULL if an error occurs. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\Hypertarget{yyjson_8c_a5755f297c3a913f7a312c2ac67be0b56}\index{yyjson.c@{yyjson.c}!yyjson\_read\_opts@{yyjson\_read\_opts}}
\index{yyjson\_read\_opts@{yyjson\_read\_opts}!yyjson.c@{yyjson.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{yyjson\_read\_opts()}{yyjson\_read\_opts()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8c_a5755f297c3a913f7a312c2ac67be0b56} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__doc}{yyjson\+\_\+doc}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} yyjson\+\_\+read\+\_\+opts (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{dat}{, }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{len}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a36af676813028c1360e8b343768f0e81}{yyjson\+\_\+read\+\_\+flag}}}]{flg}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__alc}{yyjson\+\_\+alc}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{alc}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__read__err}{yyjson\+\_\+read\+\_\+err}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{err}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Read JSON with options.

This function is thread-\/safe when\+:
\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item The {\ttfamily dat} is not modified by other threads.
\item The {\ttfamily alc} is thread-\/safe or NULL.
\end{DoxyEnumerate}


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em dat} & The JSON data (UTF-\/8 without BOM), null-\/terminator is not required. If this parameter is NULL, the function will fail and return NULL. The {\ttfamily dat} will not be modified without the flag {\ttfamily YYJSON\+\_\+\+READ\+\_\+\+INSITU}, so you can pass a {\ttfamily const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}} string and case it to {\ttfamily char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}} if you don\textquotesingle{}t use the {\ttfamily YYJSON\+\_\+\+READ\+\_\+\+INSITU} flag. \\
\hline
{\em len} & The length of JSON data in bytes. If this parameter is 0, the function will fail and return NULL. \\
\hline
{\em flg} & The JSON read options. Multiple options can be combined with {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}} operator. 0 means no options. \\
\hline
{\em alc} & The memory allocator used by JSON reader. Pass NULL to use the libc\textquotesingle{}s default allocator. \\
\hline
{\em err} & \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} pointer to receive error information. Pass NULL if you don\textquotesingle{}t need error information. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
\doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} new JSON document, or NULL if an error occurs. When it\textquotesingle{}s no longer needed, it should be freed with {\ttfamily \doxylink{yyjson_8h_adad98bd766cf52d99f2c54dcb120786d}{yyjson\+\_\+doc\+\_\+free()}}. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{yyjson\_val\_write\_file@{yyjson\_val\_write\_file}!yyjson.c@{yyjson.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{yyjson\_val\_write\_file()}{yyjson\_val\_write\_file()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8c_a2044da21f58f018ed78bb12369715be9} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} yyjson\+\_\+val\+\_\+write\+\_\+file (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{path}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__val}{yyjson\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{val}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_afb7989387fc481f678e13325c18e6338}{yyjson\+\_\+write\+\_\+flag}}}]{flg}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__alc}{yyjson\+\_\+alc}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{alc}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__write__err}{yyjson\+\_\+write\+\_\+err}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{err}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Write a value to JSON file with options.

This function is thread-\/safe when\+:
\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item The file is not accessed by other threads.
\item The {\ttfamily alc} is thread-\/safe or NULL.
\end{DoxyEnumerate}


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em path} & The JSON file\textquotesingle{}s path. If this path is NULL or invalid, the function will fail and return false. If this file is not empty, the content will be discarded. \\
\hline
{\em val} & The JSON root value. If this parameter is NULL, the function will fail and return NULL. \\
\hline
{\em flg} & The JSON write options. Multiple options can be combined with {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}} operator. 0 means no options. \\
\hline
{\em alc} & The memory allocator used by JSON writer. Pass NULL to use the libc\textquotesingle{}s default allocator. \\
\hline
{\em err} & \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} pointer to receive error information. Pass NULL if you don\textquotesingle{}t need error information. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
true if successful, false if an error occurs.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
On 32-\/bit operating system, files larger than 2GB may fail to write. 
\end{DoxyWarning}
函数调用图\+:

This table is used to convert 4 hex character sequence to a number. \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} valid hex character \mbox{[}0-\/9A-\/\+Fa-\/f\mbox{]} will mapped to it\textquotesingle{}s raw number \mbox{[}0x00, 0x0F\mbox{]}, an invalid hex character will mapped to \mbox{[}0x\+F0\mbox{]}. (generate with misc/make\+\_\+tables.\+c) \Hypertarget{yyjson_8c_a367e52eb0fd543f9e557659b26f88ddb}\index{yyjson.c@{yyjson.c}!pow10\_sig\_table@{pow10\_sig\_table}}
